***мамонт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мамонт.html>ма́монт</a> (13673)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from an <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Uralic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Uralic languages">Uralic</a></span> language, like Proto-<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mansi_language" class="extiw" title="w:Mansi language">Mansi</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="mns">*mē̮ŋ-ońt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">earth-horn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare Northern Mansi <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mns">ма</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mns-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">earth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mns">аньт</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mns-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">anʹt</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) or Khanty. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Uralic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Uralic">Proto-Uralic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="urj-pro">*mëxe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">earth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мамонт.html>ма́монт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mámont</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мамонт.html>ма́монта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мамонт.html>ма́монты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мамонт.html>ма́монтов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ма́монтовый</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mammoth</li></ol>

***манатки.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:манатки.html>мана́тки</a> (25601)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манатки.html>мана́тки</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">manátki</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манатки.html>мана́ток</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (one's) things, belongings, gear</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:манатки.html>мана́тки</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мандарин.html>мандари́н</a> (16324)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мандарин.html>мандари́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mandarín</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мандарин.html>мандари́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мандарин.html>мандари́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мандарин.html>мандари́нов</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:мандарин.html>мандари́н</a></strong></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мандари́новый</b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мандолина.html>мандоли́на</a> (30492)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мандолина.html>мандоли́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mandolína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мандолина.html>мандоли́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мандолина.html>мандоли́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мандолина.html>мандоли́н</a></b>)

***маневрировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:маневрировать.html>маневри́ровать</a> (21443)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">manœuvrer</i>, probably through <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">manövrieren</i>. Analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">манёвр</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">manjóvr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маневрировать.html>маневри́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">manevrírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сманеври́ровать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to manoeuvre, to maneuver</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to redistribute</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to manage, to use</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rail transport</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shunt</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манера.html>мане́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">manéra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манера.html>мане́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манера.html>мане́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манера.html>мане́р</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:маниакальный.html>маниака́льный</a> (17191)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">maniacal</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маниакальный.html>маниака́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maniakálʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)маниака́льнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)маниака́льней</b>)

***манипулировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:манипулировать.html>манипули́ровать</a> (23425)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">manipulieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манипулировать.html>манипули́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">manipulírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to manipulate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манипуляция.html>манипуля́ция</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">manipuljácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манипулятор.html>манипуля́тор</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">manipuljátor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ма<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>пу<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 2a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-манипул-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ир-ова</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:манипулятор.html>манипуля́тор</a> (28486)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">манипул(и́ровать)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">manipul(írovatʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́тор</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манипулятор.html>манипуля́тор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">manipuljátor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манипулятор.html>манипуля́тора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манипулятор.html>манипуля́торы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манипулятор.html>манипуля́торов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>manipulator <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">person who manipulates others</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> external pointing device <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. a mouse or trackball</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***манить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:манить.html>мани́ть</a> (7027)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*maniti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to deceive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*meh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">good, timely</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:манить.html>мани́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">manítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поманить.html>помани́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to beckon, to wave <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to attract, to lure, to entice, to allure</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мания.html>ма́ния</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mánija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мания.html>ма́нии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мания.html>ма́нии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мания.html>ма́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mania (violent derangement)</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">mansarde</i>, from a surname of French architect <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Mansart" class="extiw" title="w:François Mansart">w:François_Mansart</a>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мансарда.html>манса́рда</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mansárda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мансарда.html>манса́рды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мансарда.html>манса́рды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мансарда.html>манса́рд</a></b>)

***мануфактура.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мануфактура.html>мануфакту́ра</a> (19789)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">manufaktura</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">manufactura</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мануфактура.html>мануфакту́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">manufaktúra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мануфактура.html>мануфакту́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мануфактура.html>мануфакту́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мануфактура.html>мануфакту́р</a></b>)
</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> drapery, textiles</li></ol>
